overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-31">C_{\rm L}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> values. The lower reflection coefficient <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-32-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-222" role="math" style="width: 1.565em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.38em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-223"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-224"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-225" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-226"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-227"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-228" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">11</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-32">S_{11}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> at 500MHz corresponds to a balun resonance. Agreement between simulation and measurement is good, however some discrepancy can be observed. This is attributed to the tolerances in the lumped elements and the substrate material. In addition, <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig2" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 2</a> depicts the current distribution associated with the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-33-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-229" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-230"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-231"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-232"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-233" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-234" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-235" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-33">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode (868 MHz). Inspection of the inset reveals higher current flow around the outer loop <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-34-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-236" role="math" style="width: 1.805em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.625em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.5em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-237"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-238" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-239"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.844em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.48em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-240" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">I<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.423em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-241"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-242"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-243" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-244" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-34">(I_{1})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> in comparison to the inner loop <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-35-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-245" role="math" style="width: 1.805em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.625em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.5em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-246"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-247" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-248"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.844em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.48em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-249" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">I<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.423em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-250"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-251"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-252" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-253" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-35">(I_{2})</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The two currents are unidirectional. Moreover, even if the total perimeter of the loop is comparable to the operating wavelength, both currents <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-36-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-254" role="math" style="width: 0.964em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.844em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1000.84em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-255"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-256"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.844em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.48em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-257" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">I<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.423em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-258"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-259"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-260" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-36">I_{1}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-37-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-261" role="math" style="width: 0.964em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.844em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1000.84em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-262"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-263"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.844em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.48em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-264" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">I<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.423em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-265"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-266"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-267" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-37">I_{2}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> are uniformly distributed because the phase constant <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-38-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-268" role="math" style="width: 0.604em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.544em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1000.54em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-269"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-270"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-271"></span></span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-272" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">β<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.003em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.137em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-38">{}\beta</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is near zero.</p><p>The left-handed loop antenna is now analyzed with the capacitors that load the outer loop of the antenna replaced by varactor diodes. The resonant frequency of the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-39-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-273" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-274"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-275"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-276"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-277" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-278" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-279" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-39">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode is controlled by the loading values. Consequently, a tunable passive UHF reader loop antenna with a reconfigurable response for RFID applications can be designed. The inductors are fixed to <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-40-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-280" role="math" style="width: 4.568em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 4.087em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1004.03em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-281"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-282"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.204em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-283" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">L</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-284"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-285"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-286" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-287" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-288" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">200</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-40">L_{\rm L}=200 </script></tex-math></inline-formula>nH, but the value of the capacitors can be varied if implemented as varactor diodes. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig3" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 3</a> shows the reflection coefficient of the proposed antenna for different values of the variable capacitors.
</p><div class="figure figure-full" id="fig3"><!--          Workaround for combined images.Eg.- 1000116 Fig. 5        --><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/7727/6170612/6203553/6203553-fig-3-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/7727/6170612/6203553/6203553-fig-3-small.gif" alt="Figure 3" /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Fig. 3. </b><fig><p>Return loss of the proposed tunable-frequency passive UHF reader loop antenna.</p></fig></div><p class="links"><a href="/document/6203553/all-figures" class="all">View All</a></p></div>
<p></p><p>In between the left- and right-handed regions, we can achieve the zero <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-41-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-289" role="math" style="width: 3.607em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.246em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1003.13em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-290"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-291" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-292"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-293"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-294" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-295" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-296" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-297" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-41">({n}=0)</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode with a wide working frequency range. More specifically, the tuning range for the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-42-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-298" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-299"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-300"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-301"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-302" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-303" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-304" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-42">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode goes from 717 <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-43-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-305" role="math" style="width: 7.39em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 6.67em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1006.55em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-306"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-307" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-308"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-309" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">C<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.724em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-310"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-311"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-312" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-313" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-314" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">1.24</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-315" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;"> </span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-316"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-317"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-318"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-319"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-320" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">pF</span></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-321" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-43">(C_{\rm L}=1.24\ {\hbox{pF}})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> to 1056 MHz <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-44-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-322" role="math" style="width: 7.931em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 7.15em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1007.03em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-323"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-324" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-325"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-326" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">C<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.724em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-327"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-328"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-329" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-330" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-331" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0.475</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-332" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;"> </span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-333"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-334"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-335"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-336"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-337" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">pF</span></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-338" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-44">(C_{\rm L}=0.475\ {\hbox{pF}})</script></tex-math></inline-formula>. The antenna is well matched <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-45-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-339" role="math" style="width: 7.631em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 6.85em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1006.73em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-340"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-341" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-342"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.384em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-343" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-344"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-345"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-346" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">11</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-347" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">≤</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-348" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">−</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-349" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">10</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-350" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;"> </span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-351"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-352"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-353"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-354"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-355" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">dB</span></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-356" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-45">(S_{11}\leq-10\ {\hbox{dB}})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> for all the values. This means a tuning bandwidth of 39%. Moreover, different parameters at each shifted resonance for the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-46-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-357" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-358"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-359"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-360"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-361" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-362" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-363" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-46">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode are presented in <a ref-type="table" anchor="table1" class="fulltext-link">Table I</a>. The directivity refers to the maximum value of directivity, usually obtained in the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-47-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-364" role="math" style="width: 1.204em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.084em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.565em 1001.08em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-365"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-366" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">x</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-367" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">y<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.003em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-47">xy</script></tex-math></inline-formula>-plane for this configuration. The total efficiency <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-48-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-368" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.35em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-369"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-370" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-371" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">E</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-372" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-373"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.664em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.36em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-374" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.303em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-375"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-376"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-377" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">t</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-378" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-48">(\rm Eff_{t})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is defined as the ratio of radiated to stimulated power of the antenna. Compared to the input power, the stimulated power considers reflections occurring at the feed location. The reflection efficiency <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-49-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-379" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.35em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-380"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-381" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-382" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">E</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-383" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-384"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.664em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.36em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-385" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">f<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.303em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-386"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-387"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-388" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">r</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-389" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-49">(\rm Eff_{r})</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is defined as the ratio of input to stimulated power. Note that the input power is the accepted power, i.e., reflected power and power flowing out any port of the simulated structure are not included.
</p><div class="figure figure-full table" id="table1"><div class="figcaption"><b class="title">Table I </b>Study of the Frequency-Tunable UHF Loop Antenna Working at the <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-50-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-390" role="math" style="width: 2.847em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.252em; height: 0px; font-size: 126%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.392em 1002.19em 2.45em -999.997em); top: -2.245em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-391"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-392"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-393"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-394" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-395" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.268em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-396" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.268em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.252em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.079em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.004em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-50">{n}=0</script> Mode<div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></div><div class="img-wrap"><a href="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/7727/6170612/6203553/6203553-table-1-large.gif"><img src="/mediastore/IEEE/content/media/7727/6170612/6203553/6203553-table-1-small.gif" alt="Table " /><div class="zoom" title="View Larger Image"></div></a></div></div>
<p></p><p>The results show that variation of the capacitor <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-51-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-397" role="math" style="width: 1.444em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.26em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-398"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-399"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-400" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">C<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.724em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-401"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-402"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-403" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-51">C_{\rm L}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> gives rise to frequency shifts and a modification of antenna efficiency, directivity, and input impedance. Increasing or decreasing the value of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-52-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-404" role="math" style="width: 1.444em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.26em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-405"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-406"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.264em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-407" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">C<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.724em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-408"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-409"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-410" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-52">C_{\rm L}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> yields lower or higher resonant frequencies, efficiency, and input impedance, respectively. Directivity remains almost constant, and it is always above 2 dBi within the capacitance values under investigation. For the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-53-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-411" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-412"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-413"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-414"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-415" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-416" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-417" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-53">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode, the variation of the load inductance <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-54-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-418" role="math" style="width: 1.324em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.204em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.2em 2.465em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-419"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-420"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.204em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-421" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">L</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-422"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-423"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-424" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-54">L_{\rm L}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> does not have a strong influence on the properties analyzed. This can be explained by the small current that flows through these elements (see inset of <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig2" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 2</a>).</p><p>A reconfigurable-pattern passive UHF reader loop antenna for RFID applications has also been designed. The antenna parameters are defined in the caption of <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig1" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 1</a>. However, in this design, a loading inductance of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-55-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-425" role="math" style="width: 4.568em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 4.087em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1004.03em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-426"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-427"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.204em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-428" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">L</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.664em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-429"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-430"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-431" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">L</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-432" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-433" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">450</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.197em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-55">L_{\rm L}=450 </script></tex-math></inline-formula>nH and a distance between wires <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-56-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-434" role="math" style="width: 3.246em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.886em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.83em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-435"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-436"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-437"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-438" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">d<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.003em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-439" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-440" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">19</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-56">{d}=19 </script></tex-math></inline-formula>mm have been employed. It has been found through extensive simulations that different mode numbers, namely <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-57-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-441" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-442"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-443"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-444"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-445" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-446" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-447" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-57">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-58-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-448" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-449"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-450"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-451"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-452" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-453" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-454" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">2</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-58">{n}=2</script></tex-math></inline-formula> modes, can be obtained at the RFID frequency with two different loading capacitors. Therefore, a passive UHF reader loop antenna with very different properties can be obtained. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig4" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 4</a> shows the simulated return loss characteristic in amplitude with the two selected capacitance values. The resonant frequency of each mode is controlled by the loading capacitors. In particular, the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-59-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-455" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-456"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-457"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-458"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-459" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-460" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-461" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">0</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-59">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode was achieved with loading capacitances equal to 0.7 pF as shown by the solid line. Another value of 30 pF was chosen for the loading capacitors to obtain the same resonance frequency at mode number <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-60-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-462" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-463"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-464"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-465"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-466" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-467" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-468" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">2</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-60">{n}=2</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, as shown by the dashed line. <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig5" class="fulltext-link">Fig. 5</a> shows the far-field radiation pattern obtained for the two operating modes. It can be found that the loop gives an omnidirectional pattern in the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-61-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-469" role="math" style="width: 1.204em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.084em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.565em 1001.08em 2.526em -999.997em); overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.003em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-61">xy</script></tex-math></inline-formula>-plane with a null along the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-62-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-473" role="math" style="width: 0.544em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.483em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.565em 1000.48em 2.345em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-474"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-475" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">z<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.003em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.67em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-62">z</script></tex-math></inline-formula>-axis while working in an <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-63-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-476" role="math" style="width: 2.766em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-477"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-478"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-479"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-480" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-481" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-63">{n}=0</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode. The antenna can switch to a pattern with two main lobes on the <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="TeX"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-64-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-483" role="math" style="width: 0.544em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.483em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.565em 1000.48em 2.345em -999.997em); display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.465em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1002.4em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-487"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-488"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-489"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-490" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">n</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-491" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-492" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">2</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.87em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-65">{n}=2</script></tex-math></inline-formula> mode. An RFID antenna with orthogonal radiation patterns, and therefore with almost an isotropic covering area, can be achieved.
